title="Manufacturing Advisory Service">Manufacturing Advisory Service</a> for the region is based on the <a href="/wiki/A606_road" title="A606 road">A606</a> in <a href="/wiki/Melton_Mowbray" title="Melton Mowbray">Melton Mowbray</a>, next to <a href="/wiki/East_Midlands_Councils" title="East Midlands Councils">East Midlands Councils</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manufacturing">Manufacturing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Midlands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Manufacturing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_070804-N-1745W-122_A_Sailor_assigned_to_Aircraft_Intermediate_Maintenance_Department_(AIMD)_tests_an_aircraft_jet_engine_for_defects_while_performing_Jet_Engine_Test_Instrumentation,_(JETI)_Certification-Engine_Runs.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/US_Navy_070804-N-1745W-122_A_Sailor_assigned_to_Aircraft_Intermediate_Maintenance_Department_%28AIMD%29_tests_an_aircraft_jet_engine_for_defects_while_performing_Jet_Engine_Test_Instrumentation%2C_%28JETI%29_Certification-Engine_Runs.jpg/220px-thumbnail.jpg" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/US_Navy_070804-N-1745W-122_A_Sailor_assigned_to_Aircraft_Intermediate_Maintenance_Department_%28AIMD%29_tests_an_aircraft_jet_engine_for_defects_while_performing_Jet_Engine_Test_Instrumentation%2C_%28JETI%29_Certification-Engine_Runs.jpg/330px-thumbnail.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/US_Navy_070804-N-1745W-122_A_Sailor_assigned_to_Aircraft_Intermediate_Maintenance_Department_%28AIMD%29_tests_an_aircraft_jet_engine_for_defects_while_performing_Jet_Engine_Test_Instrumentation%2C_%28JETI%29_Certification-Engine_Runs.jpg/440px-thumbnail.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2100" data-file-height="1500" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_070804-N-1745W-122_A_Sailor_assigned_to_Aircraft_Intermediate_Maintenance_Department_(AIMD)_tests_an_aircraft_jet_engine_for_defects_while_performing_Jet_Engine_Test_Instrumentation,_(JETI)_Certification-Engine_Runs.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Jet_engine" title="Jet engine">jet engine</a> was built and <a href="/wiki/Power_Jets" title="Power Jets">developed</a> in the region</div></div></div>\n<p>In 2003, 23% of economic output in the East Midlands was in manufacturing, compared to 15% in the UK.\n</p><p>For engineering, <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_plc" class="mw-redirect" title="Rolls-Royce plc">Rolls-Royce</a> (the world\'s second-largest maker of <a href="/wiki/Aircraft_engine" title="Aircraft engine">aero engines</a>) in <a href="/wiki/Sinfin" title="Sinfin">Sinfin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Marine_Power_Operations" title="Rolls-Royce Marine Power Operations">Rolls-Royce Marine Power Operations</a> are both in Derby. <a href="/wiki/Ruston_(engine_builder)" title="Ruston (engine builder)">Siemens Industrial Turbomachinery</a> (former <a href="/wiki/General_Electric_Company_plc" class="mw-redirect" title="General Electric Company plc">GEC</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Alstom" title="Alstom">Alstom</a>) make industrial <a href="/wiki/Gas_turbine" title="Gas turbine">gas turbines</a> in Lincoln, with a former division making aero-engine components now part of <a href="/wiki/Industria_de_Turbo_Propulsores" title="Industria de Turbo Propulsores">ITP Engines</a> UK, based at <a href="/wiki/Whetstone,_Leicestershire" title="Whetstone, Leicestershire">Whetstone</a>, next door to <a href="/wiki/Hardinge,_Inc." title="Hardinge, Inc.">Hardinge</a> Machine Tools UK (former <a href="/wiki/Bridgeport_(machine_tool_brand)" title="Bridgeport (machine tool brand)">Bridgeport</a>). <a href="/wiki/Cytec_Industries" title="Cytec Industries">Cytec Industries</a> UK (former <a href="/w/index.php?title=Uneco&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Uneco (page does not exist)">Uneco</a>, owned since 2016 by <a href="/wiki/Solvay_S.A." title="Solvay S.A.">Solvay</a>) have a composites research centre in the south of Heanor. <a href="/wiki/Meggitt" class="mw-redirect" title="Meggitt">Meggitt</a> Polymers &amp; Composites (former Dunlop) are on the A512 in Shepshed, who make seals for aircraft.\n</p>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Motorsport_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Motorsport in the United Kingdom">Motorsport in the United Kingdom</a></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Triumph_Motorcycles_Ltd" title="Triumph Motorcycles Ltd">Triumph Motorcycles</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ultima_Sports" title="Ultima Sports">Ultima Sports</a> (<a href="/wiki/Sports_car" title="Sports car">sports cars</a>) are in <a href="/wiki/Hinckley" title="Hinckley">Hinckley</a>. <a href="/wiki/Cummins" title="Cummins">Cummins</a> make diesel engines in <a href="/wiki/Daventry" title="Daventry">Daventry</a>, and build <a href="/wiki/Alternating_current" title="Alternating current">AC</a> <a href="/wiki/Alternator" title="Alternator">generators</a> in <a href="/wiki/Stamford,_Lincolnshire" title="Stamford, Lincolnshire">Stamford</a>, with its spares division at Wellingborough (near Mahle). 80% of the world\'s <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> cars are made in Northamptonshire. At the north of Motorsport Valley, <a href="/wiki/Cosworth" title="Cosworth">Cosworth</a> and <a href="/wiki/MAHLE_Powertrain" title="MAHLE Powertrain">MAHLE Powertrain</a> (former Cosworth Technology before January 2005) are next to the Nene in Northampton, with an <a href="/wiki/Cylinder_block" title="Cylinder block">engine block</a> plant off the <a href="/wiki/A509_road" title="A509 road">A509</a> in Wellingborough. <a href="/wiki/Force_India" title="Force India">Force India</a> and <a href="/wiki/Delta_Motorsport" title="Delta Motorsport">Delta Motorsport</a> are at <a href="/wiki/Silverstone" title="Silverstone">Silverstone</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mercedes_AMG_High_Performance_Powertrains" title="Mercedes AMG High Performance Powertrains">Mercedes AMG High Performance Powertrains</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Brixworth" title="Brixworth">Brixworth</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes-Benz in Formula One</a> at Brackley at the A43/<a href="/wiki/A422_road" title="A422 road">A422</a> roundabout. Near Leicester, <a href="/wiki/Noble_Automotive" title="Noble Automotive">Noble</a> are in <a href="/wiki/Barwell" title="Barwell">Barwell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fenix_Automotive" title="Fenix Automotive">Fenix Automotive</a> in Braunstone. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Eibach_Federn&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Eibach Federn (page does not exist)">Eibach Federn</a> UK (shock absorbers) is off the B581 in <a href="/wiki/Broughton_Astley" title="Broughton Astley">Broughton Astley</a>. <a href="/wiki/KTM" title="KTM">KTM</a> UK (high-performance motorcycles) is at Buckingham Industrial Estate in southeast Brackley next to the A43; to the west, next door over the <a href="/wiki/Banbury_to_Verney_Junction_Branch_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Banbury to Verney Junction Branch Line">former railway</a> was <a href="/wiki/Brawn_GP" title="Brawn GP">Brawn GP</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Honda_in_Formula_One" title="Honda in Formula One">Honda F1</a> before 2008) near the A422 roundabout in <a href="/wiki/Evenley" title="Evenley">Evenley</a>.  <a href="/wiki/Van_Hool" title="Van Hool">Van Hool</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Coachbuilder" title="Coachbuilder">coachwork</a>) is on Finedon Road Industrial Estate in Wellingborough.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Salvador_Caetano" title="Salvador Caetano">Caetano</a> UK is based near Coalville, a UK coachwork distributor for many coaches, often <a href="/wiki/National_Express_Coaches" title="National Express Coaches">National Express</a>. <a href="/wiki/AGC_Glass_Europe" title="AGC Glass Europe">AGC Automotive UK</a> (<a href="/wiki/Asahi_Glass_Co." class="mw-redirect" title="Asahi Glass Co.">Asahi Glass Co.</a>) make <a href="/wiki/Car_glass" class="mw-redirect" title="Car glass">automotive glass</a> (<a href="/wiki/Toughened_glass" class="mw-redirect" title="Toughened glass">tempered glass</a> and <a href="/wiki/Laminated_glass" title="Laminated glass">laminated glass</a>) on <a href="/wiki/Round_Spinney" title="Round Spinney">Round Spinney</a> Ind Est in the north of Northampton. <a href="/wiki/Plastic_Omnium" title="Plastic Omnium">Plastic Omnium</a> Automotive make automotive exteriors in the west of Measham. Off the <a href="/wiki/A361_road" title="A361 road">A361</a> on a former <a href="/wiki/RAF_Chipping_Warden" title="RAF Chipping Warden">airfield</a> is a manufacturing site of <a href="/wiki/Lippstadt" title="Lippstadt">Lippstadt</a>-based <a href="/wiki/Hella_(company)" title="Hella (company)">Hella</a> UK (LED automobile lighting, and Europe\'s largest automobile lighting manufacturer) in <a href="/wiki/Chipping_Warden" title="Chipping Warden">Chipping Warden</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aston_le_Walls" title="Aston le Walls">Aston le Walls</a>, close to the Oxfordshire boundary. <a href="/wiki/Ilmor" title="Ilmor">Ilmor</a> is in Brixworth, and <a href="/wiki/Bowler_Offroad" title="Bowler Offroad">Bowler Offroad</a> is in Belper.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/J._C._Bamford" class="mw-redirect" title="J. C. Bamford">JCB</a> Power Systems is on an <a href="/w/index.php?title=RAF_Church_Broughton&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="RAF Church Broughton (page does not exist)">old airfield</a> near <a href="/wiki/Foston,_Derbyshire" title="Foston, Derbyshire">Foston, Derbyshire</a> and nearby <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Manufacturing_UK" title="Toyota Manufacturing UK">Toyota Manufacturing UK</a> (TMUK) is on an <a href="/wiki/RAF_Burnaston" class="mw-redirect" title="RAF Burnaston">old airfield</a> at <a href="/wiki/Burnaston" title="Burnaston">Burnaston</a>, where its 3,000 employees make the <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Auris" title="Toyota Auris">Auris</a> and <a href="/wiki/Toyota_Avensis" title="Toyota Avensis">Avensis</a>, making 190,000 in 2015. <a href="/wiki/Resonate_Group" title="Resonate Group">Resonate Group</a> (former DeltaRail Group) is in Derby, and <a href="/wiki/Bombardier_Transportation" title="Bombardier Transportation">Bombardier UK</a> (former <a href="/wiki/British_Rail_Engineering_Limited" title="British Rail Engineering Limited">British Rail Engineering Limited</a> before 1996 then <a href="/wiki/Adtranz" title="Adtranz">ABB Adtranz</a>) is Britain\'s only <a href="/w/index.php?title=Derby_Carriage_Litchurch_Lane_Works&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Derby Carriage Litchurch Lane Works (page does not exist)">train manufacturer</a> left, and is in <a href="/wiki/Litchurch" title="Litchurch">Litchurch</a>; it built the <a href="/wiki/Nottingham" title="Nottingham">Nottingham Express Transit</a> <a href="/wiki/AT6/5" class="mw-redirect" title="AT6/5">trams</a> in 2004, the <a href="/wiki/Electrostar" title="Electrostar">Electrostar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Turbostar" title="Turbostar">Turbostar</a> fleet, and <a href="/wiki/London_Underground_rolling_stock" title="London Underground rolling stock">London Underground trains</a>. South of the factory is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Pattonair&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Pattonair (page does not exist)">Pattonair</a>, a global aircraft components supplier. <a href="/wiki/APPH" title="APPH">APPH</a> (part of <a href="/wiki/BBA_Aviation" title="BBA Aviation">BBA Aviation</a>) make aircraft <a href="/wiki/Landing_gear" title="Landing gear">landing gear</a> on the B6020 next to <a href="/wiki/Kirkby-in-Ashfield_railway_station" title="Kirkby-in-Ashfield railway station">Kirkby-in-Ashfield railway station</a>. <a href="/wiki/Raleigh_Bicycle_Company" title="Raleigh Bicycle Company">Raleigh Bicycle Company</a> is based in New <a href="/wiki/Eastwood,_Nottinghamshire" title="Eastwood, Nottinghamshire">Eastwood</a> next to the A610; its former site on Triumph Road is now the quirkily designed <a href="/wiki/Campuses_of_the_University_of_Nottingham" title="Campuses of the University of Nottingham">Jubilee Campus</a> of the University of Nottingham which has the UK\'s tallest sculpture (52&#160;m, 171&#160;ft, <i><a href="/wiki/Aspire_(sculpture)" title="Aspire (sculpture)">Aspire</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Essentra_Packaging" title="Essentra Packaging">Essentra Packaging</a> (former Payne) nearby in Giltbrook, next to A610 near the A6096/B6010 junction next to <a href="/wiki/IKEA" title="IKEA">IKEA</a>, makes <a href="/wiki/Tear_tape" title="Tear tape">tear tape</a>, owned by <a href="/wiki/Essentra" title="Essentra">Essentra</a>, former <a href="/wiki/Filtrona" class="mw-redirect" title="Filtrona">Filtrona</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Beamlight_Automotive_Seating&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Beamlight Automotive Seating (page does not exist)">Beamlight Automotive Seating</a> (former site of <a href="/wiki/Magna_International" title="Magna International">Magna Seating Systems</a>) is nearby. <a href="/wiki/Giant_Bicycles" title="Giant Bicycles">Giant</a> UK (high performance bicycles) on the Charnwood Edge Business Park at the A46/A607 junction in <a href="/wiki/Cossington,_Leicestershire" title="Cossington, Leicestershire">Cossington</a> near the Midland Main Line and <a href="/wiki/River_Wreake" title="River Wreake">River Wreake</a>. <a href="/wiki/Mettler_Toledo" title="Mettler Toledo">Mettler Toledo</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Beltweigher" title="Beltweigher">industrial weighing</a>) is in the west of Beaumont Leys.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Ferodo" title="Ferodo">Ferodo</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Chapel-en-le-Frith" title="Chapel-en-le-Frith">Chapel-en-le-Frith</a>, who have made <a href="/wiki/Brake_pad" title="Brake pad">brake pads</a> since its founder <a href="/wiki/Herbert_Frood" title="Herbert Frood">Herbert Frood</a> invented them in <a href="/wiki/Combs,_Derbyshire" title="Combs, Derbyshire">Combs</a> in 1897. <a href="/wiki/Carbolite" class="mw-redirect" title="Carbolite">Carbolite</a>, which makes industrial furnaces, is based near the B6049/A6187 junction in the <a href="/wiki/Hope_Valley,_Derbyshire" title="Hope Valley, Derbyshire">Hope Valley</a>. FRAM Industrial (former Eurofilter and part of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Champion_Laboratories&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Champion Laboratories (page does not exist)">Champion Laboratories</a>, then <a href="/w/index.php?title=UCI-FRAM_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="UCI-FRAM Group (page does not exist)">UCI-FRAM Group</a>) make air filters for <a href="/wiki/Gas_turbine" title="Gas turbine">gas turbines</a> in Mansfield on Crown Farm Industrial Estate.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Harworth_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_104989.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Harworth_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_104989.jpg/220px-Harworth_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_104989.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Harworth_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_104989.jpg/330px-Harworth_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_104989.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Harworth_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_104989.jpg/440px-Harworth_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_104989.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="427" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Harworth_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_104989.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/UK_Coal" title="UK Coal">UK Coal</a> (formerly RJB Mining) was based in <a href="/wiki/Styrrup" title="Styrrup">Styrrup</a> near <a href="/wiki/Harworth" title="Harworth">Harworth</a>. The north part of Derbyshire and Nottinghamshire used to have many <a href="/wiki/Coal_mining" title="Coal mining">coal mines</a>, and the last two pits producing in Nottinghamshire were near <a href="/wiki/Market_Warsop" class="mw-redirect" title="Market Warsop">Market Warsop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thoresby_Colliery" title="Thoresby Colliery">Ollerton</a></div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/FKI_(company)" title="FKI (company)">FKI</a> who own <a href="/wiki/Brush_Electrical_Machines" title="Brush Electrical Machines">Brush Electrical Machines</a> is in Loughborough, home to the <a href="/wiki/Energy_Technologies_Institute" title="Energy Technologies Institute">Energy Technologies Institute</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_Taylor_%26_Co" title="John Taylor &amp; Co">John Taylor &amp; Co</a>, which although entering <a href="/wiki/Administration_(law)" title="Administration (law)">administration</a> in 2009, is the largest <a href="/wiki/Bellfounding" title="Bellfounding">bell foundry</a> in the world. <a href="/wiki/Eco-Bat_Technologies" title="Eco-Bat Technologies">Eco-Bat Technologies</a>, based in <a href="/w/index.php?title=South_Darley&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="South Darley (page does not exist)">South Darley</a>, west of <a href="/wiki/Matlock,_Derbyshire" title="Matlock, Derbyshire">Matlock</a>, <a href="/wiki/Smelting" title="Smelting">smelt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Derbyshire_lead_mining_history" title="Derbyshire lead mining history">mine lead</a>, and are the world\'s biggest producer of <a href="/wiki/Lead" title="Lead">lead</a>, and own eighteen sites across the world. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Doff_Portland&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Doff Portland (page does not exist)">Doff Portland</a>, off the A611 at Hucknall, make horticultural pesticides such as <a href="/wiki/Molluscicide" title="Molluscicide">slug killer</a>. <a href="/wiki/Dow_Chemical_Company" title="Dow Chemical Company">Dow</a> <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperlast&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hyperlast (page does not exist)">Hyperlast</a> makes <a href="/wiki/Polyurethane" title="Polyurethane">polyurethane</a> products off the <a href="/wiki/A6015_road_(Great_Britain)" class="mw-redirect" title="A6015 road (Great Britain)">A6015</a> at <a href="/wiki/Birch_Vale" title="Birch Vale">Birch Vale</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hayfield" title="Hayfield">Hayfield</a> in north-west Derbyshire, next to the <a href="/wiki/River_Sett" title="River Sett">River Sett</a>. <a href="/wiki/Scott_Bader" class="mw-redirect" title="Scott Bader">Scott Bader</a> develop and manufacture <a href="/wiki/Polyester_resin" title="Polyester resin">polyester resins</a> for glass-reinforced plastic (<a href="/wiki/Fiberglass" title="Fiberglass">fiberglass</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Gelcoat" title="Gelcoat">gelcoats</a>) at <a In Worksop near the A60/A57 roundabout <a href="/w/index.php?title=Cinch_Connectors&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cinch Connectors (page does not exist)">Cinch Connectors</a> (part of <a href="/wiki/Safran" title="Safran">Safran</a>) have their European plant, making <a href="/wiki/D-subminiature" title="D-subminiature">D-subminiature</a> connectors (found on the back of computers); on the Dukeries Industrial Estate, Worksop Galvanizers (<a href="/wiki/Wedge_Group" title="Wedge Group">Wedge Group</a>) have the largest <a href="/wiki/Galvanization" title="Galvanization">galvanizing bath</a> (zinc) in the UK, able to fit up to 29 metres in length. <a href="/wiki/Cooper_Industries" title="Cooper Industries">Cooper Bussmann</a> (former Hawker Fusegear) makes <a href="/wiki/Fuse_(electrical)" title="Fuse (electrical)">electrical fuses</a> in <a href="/wiki/Burton_on_the_Wolds" title="Burton on the Wolds">Burton on the Wolds</a> off the B676. Pearce Signs, one of the UK\'s largest sign-makers, is based in <a href="/wiki/Basford,_Nottinghamshire" class="mw-redirect" title="Basford, Nottinghamshire">New Basford</a>. Nylacast is an international <a href="/wiki/Plastics_engineering" title="Plastics engineering">engineered plastics</a> company based in <a href="/wiki/Humberstone_%26_Hamilton" title="Humberstone &amp; Hamilton">Humberstone</a>, Leicester. <a href="/wiki/Sapa_Group" class="mw-redirect" title="Sapa Group">Sapa</a> are at Tibshelf on the B6014, on the Saw Pit Lane Industrial Estate with Storetec, the UK base of <a href="/wiki/Wanzl_(Company)" title="Wanzl (Company)">Wanzl</a> shopping trolleys. At the A563 roundabout <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Land_%26_Armaments" title="BAE Systems Land &amp; Armaments">BAE Systems Land &amp; Armaments</a> had a tank factory, which closed in May 2011 when it lost the <a href="/wiki/Future_Rapid_Effect_System" title="Future Rapid Effect System">FRES</a> contract, given to General Dynamics; the site, owned by Thales, initially made naval radar systems. title="Long Buckby railway station">Long Buckby railway station</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lappset&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lappset (page does not exist)">Lappset</a> UK (play equipment) is on Telford Way in Kettering; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wicksteed_Playscapes&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Wicksteed Playscapes (page does not exist)">Wicksteed Playscapes</a> are a main manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Playground" title="Playground">playground</a> equipment in the UK, for many decades at Kettering; the company invented the equipment too. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Abbott_%26_Co.(Newark)_Ltd&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Abbott &amp; Co.(Newark) Ltd (page does not exist)">Abbott &amp; Co.(Newark) Ltd</a>, Established in 1870 and based in The Newark Boiler Works on Northern Road, Newark, made boilers in the 1870s for the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> and today design and build a large range <a href="/wiki/Pressure_vessel" title="Pressure vessel">pressure vessels</a>, some of which were used recently on <a href="/wiki/HMS_Queen_Elizabeth_(R08)" title="HMS Queen Elizabeth (R08)">HMS Queen Elizabeth (R08)</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Taylor,_Taylor_%26_Hobson_advert,_1925.jpeg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/d3/Taylor%2C_Taylor_%26_Hobson_advert%2C_1925.jpeg/220px-Taylor%2C_Taylor_%26_Hobson_advert%2C_1925.jpeg" width="220" height="338" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/d3/Taylor%2C_Taylor_%26_Hobson_advert%2C_1925.jpeg/330px-Taylor%2C_Taylor_%26_Hobson_advert%2C_1925.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/d3/Taylor%2C_Taylor_%26_Hobson_advert%2C_1925.jpeg/440px-Taylor%2C_Taylor_%26_Hobson_advert%2C_1925.jpeg 2x" data-file-width="760" data-file-height="1169" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Taylor,_Taylor_%26_Hobson_advert,_1925.jpeg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Taylor, Taylor &amp; Hobson 1925 advert</div></div></div>\n<p>Spector Lumenex (part of <a href="/wiki/Tyco_International" title="Tyco International">Tyco</a>) make warning systems off the B684 in <a href="/wiki/Mapperley" title="Mapperley">Mapperley</a>. <a href="/wiki/Flowserve" title="Flowserve">Flowserve</a> UK (former <a href="/wiki/Worthington-Simpson" title="Worthington-Simpson">Worthington-Simpson</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Ingersoll_Rand" title="Ingersoll Rand">Ingersoll-Dresser</a>) in Balderton are the largest manufacturer of industrial pumps in the UK. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Miflex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Miflex (page does not exist)">Miflex</a>, off the B582 in <a href="/wiki/Lubbesthorpe" title="Lubbesthorpe">Lubbesthorpe</a> between Enderby and Kirby Muxloe, make <a href="/w/index.php?title=Air_hose&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Air hose (page does not exist)">air hoses</a> for <a href="/wiki/Diving_regulator" title="Diving regulator">diving regulators</a>. <a href="/wiki/Hako_GmbH" title="Hako GmbH">Hako</a> Machines UK, a <a href="/wiki/Schleswig-Holstein" title="Schleswig-Holstein">Schleswig-Holstein</a> supplier of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Industrial_sweeper&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Industrial sweeper (page does not exist)">industrial sweepers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Street_sweeper" title="Street sweeper">road cleaners</a> are in Crick. <a href="/wiki/Bostik" title="Bostik">Bostik</a>, which from 1930 until 1990, was owned by <a href="/wiki/British_United_Shoe_Machinery" title="British United Shoe Machinery">British United Shoe Machinery</a> of Leicester, still has a main factory and research site (its construction division) in Belgrave; until 1962 it was made by <a href="/w/index.php?title=B._B._Chemical&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="B. B. Chemical (page does not exist)">B. B. Chemical</a>, with its other main brand being the water-resistant <a href="/wiki/Prestik" title="Prestik">Prestik</a> for making <a href="/w/index.php?title=Sealing_strip&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sealing strip (page does not exist)">sealing strips</a>. <a href="/wiki/Taylor_Hobson" title="Taylor Hobson">Taylor Hobson</a> (an international metrology company) is north of the A563 in former Thurmaston (inside Leicester), bought by <a href="/wiki/Ametek" title="Ametek">Ametek</a> in 2004; with a former division of the company, Cooke Optics, a camera lens manufacturer, further north in Thurmaston on the west side of the railway. The <a href="/wiki/Gents%27_of_Leicester" title="Gents&#39; of Leicester">Gent</a> fire alarm company, now owned by Honeywell since 2005, is off the A563 near the A6030 roundabout in the north of Humberstone. <a href="/wiki/Matsuura_Machinery" title="Matsuura Machinery">Matsuura Machinery</a> UK (CNC <a href="/wiki/Machine_tool" title="Machine tool">machine tools</a>) is towards Morrisons in Coalville. \n</p><p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Abacus_Lighting&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Abacus Lighting (page does not exist)">Abacus Lighting</a> (former Abacus Municipal) is in the north of Kirkby in Ashfield, north of Sutton Parkway station; it makes <a href="/wiki/Street_light" title="Street light">street lights</a>, <a href="/wiki/Floodlights_(sport)" class="mw-redirect" title="Floodlights (sport)">floodlights</a>, supermarket <a href="/w/index.php?title=Trolley_shelter&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Trolley shelter (page does not exist)">trolley shelters</a>, and installed many of the UK\'s <a href="/wiki/Cell_site" title="Cell site">mobile phone masts</a>. <a href="/wiki/Ardagh_Group" title="Ardagh Group">Ardagh</a> (originally <a href="/wiki/Novar_plc" title="Novar plc">Metal Box</a> from 1962, then Impress Group) make <a href="/wiki/Tin_can" title="Tin can">tin cans</a> south of the A38, off the B6139, north of Fabrikat; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Alpha_Rail&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Alpha Rail (page does not exist)">Alpha Rail</a>, off the B6020 near <a href="/wiki/Kirkby-in-Ashfield_railway_station" title="Kirkby-in-Ashfield railway station">Kirkby-in-Ashfield railway station</a>, claims to be Britain\'s leading manufacturer of metal railings and <a href="/wiki/Guard_rail" title="Guard rail">guard rail</a>; <a href="/wiki/Pandrol" title="Pandrol">Pandrol</a> UK in Worksop make resilient <a href="/wiki/Rail_fastening_system" title="Rail fastening system">rail fastenings</a>. <a href="/wiki/ThyssenKrupp_Elevator" class="mw-redirect" title="ThyssenKrupp Elevator">ThyssenKrupp Elevator</a> UK is in Lenton, off the A52, and further north is <a href="/wiki/ZF_Friedrichshafen" title="ZF Friedrichshafen">ZF Services UK</a> (wind turbine and automotive gears). At the A6019/A453 south of the tax office in Nottingham is <a href="/wiki/Thomas_%26_Betts" title="Thomas &amp; Betts">Thomas &amp; Betts</a> UK (former <a href="/w/index.php?title=W_%26_J_Furse&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="W &amp; J Furse (page does not exist)">W &amp; J Furse</a>, and bought by <a href="/wiki/ABB_Group" title="ABB Group">ABB</a> in 2012), a world leader in <a href="/wiki/Surge_protector" title="Surge protector">lightning</a> and <a href="/wiki/Earthing_system" title="Earthing system">earthing protection</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Construction_and_building_materials">Construction and building materials</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Midlands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Construction and building materials">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Topps_Tiles" title="Topps Tiles">Topps Tiles</a> are on <a href="/w/index.php?title=Grove_Park,_Leicestershire&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Grove Park, Leicestershire (page does not exist)">Grove Park</a> in Enderby, with the national distribution centre of British Gas, the largest warehouse of gas spare parts in Europe, next door. <a href="/wiki/Aggregate_Industries" title="Aggregate Industries">Aggregate Industries</a> (now part of <a href="/wiki/LafargeHolcim" title="LafargeHolcim">LafargeHolcim</a> since July 2015, when Paris-based Lafarge merged with Swiss-based Holcim) is based at Bardon Hall in <a href="/wiki/Bardon,_Leicestershire" title="Bardon, Leicestershire">Bardon</a>, next to the 912-foot (278 m) <a href="/wiki/Bardon_Hill" title="Bardon Hill">Bardon Hill</a>, Leicestershire\'s highest point. <a href="/wiki/Mountsorrel" title="Mountsorrel">Mountsorrel</a> has the largest <a href="/wiki/Granite" title="Granite">granite</a> quarry in Europe, owned by the French company, <a href="/wiki/Lafarge_(company)" title="Lafarge (company)">Lafarge</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/Redland_plc" title="Redland plc">Redland plc</a> until 1997). <a href="/wiki/BPB_plc" title="BPB plc">BPB plc</a> (British Plasterboard), the world\'s largest manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Drywall" title="Drywall">plasterboard</a> (<a href="/wiki/Calcium_sulfate" title="Calcium sulfate">calcium sulphate</a>) who own <a href="/wiki/British_Gypsum" class="mw-redirect" title="British Gypsum">British Gypsum</a>, is based in <a href="/wiki/East_Leake" title="East Leake">East Leake</a>, Nottinghamshire. They also have a large site at <a href="/wiki/Barrow_upon_Soar" title="Barrow upon Soar">Barrow upon Soar</a>. <a href="/wiki/Artex_Ltd." title="Artex Ltd.">Artex Ltd.</a>, part of the same company, is in <a href="/wiki/Ruddington" title="Ruddington">Ruddington</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=North_Midland_Construction&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="North Midland Construction (page does not exist)">North Midland Construction</a> is off the B6027 in <a href="/wiki/Huthwaite" title="Huthwaite">Huthwaite</a>. Saint-Gobain Isover (insulation) is in Gotham.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Hormann_Group" title="Hormann Group">H\xc3\xb6rmann Group</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Garage_door" title="Garage door">garage doors</a>) is in Coalville, off the A511. <a href="/wiki/Barratt_Developments" title="Barratt Developments">Barratt Developments</a> (housing) is at the <a href="/wiki/A511_road" title="A511 road">A511</a>/B585 roundabout in <a href="/wiki/Ellistown_and_Battleflat" title="Ellistown and Battleflat">Ellistown and Battleflat</a> (Bardon), southeast of Coalville; <a href="/wiki/Ibstock_plc" title="Ibstock plc">Ibstock</a> is the largest brick manufacturer (900&#160;million a year, with twenty factories) in the UK, nearby to the southwest; . <a href="/wiki/Lafarge_Tarmac" class="mw-redirect" title="Lafarge Tarmac">Lafarge Aggregates &amp; Concrete UK</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Syston" title="Syston">Syston</a>, next to the <a href="/wiki/A607_road" title="A607 road">A607</a>. <a href="/wiki/Roca_(company)" title="Roca (company)">Roca</a> UK and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Laufen_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Laufen (company) (page does not exist)">Laufen</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Plumbing_fixture" title="Plumbing fixture">sanitaryware</a>) are in the north of Coalville, next to the A511 on the Hermitage Industrial Estate, towards <a href="/wiki/Stephenson_College,_Coalville" title="Stephenson College, Coalville">Stephenson College</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Goodwin_Barsby&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Goodwin Barsby (page does not exist)">Goodwin Barsby</a> make stone <a href="/wiki/Crusher" title="Crusher">crushers</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Krohne&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Krohne (page does not exist)">Krohne</a> UK at Wellingborough make <a href="/wiki/Coriolis_effect" class="mw-redirect" title="Coriolis effect">Coriolis</a> mass <a href="/wiki/Flow_measurement" title="Flow measurement">flowmeters</a>. The <a href="/wiki/BSS_Group" class="mw-redirect" title="BSS Group">BSS Group</a> (formerly in Leicester), at the same site as <a href="/wiki/Travis_Perkins" title="Travis Perkins">Travis Perkins</a> (owner of the <a href="/wiki/Wickes" title="Wickes">Wickes</a> brand)  in north Northampton. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Flogas&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Flogas (page does not exist)">Flogas</a> (butane supplier, owned by <a href="/wiki/DCC_Plc" class="mw-redirect" title="DCC Plc">DCC</a>) is on Watermead Business Park off the A607 in west Syston near Lafarge (Granite House). <a href="/w/index.php?title=CPL_Industries&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="CPL Industries (page does not exist)">CPL Industries</a> with a site off the A61 in Wingerworth, are the UK\'s biggest manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Smokeless_fuel" title="Smokeless fuel">smokeless fuel</a>. <a href="/wiki/AvantiGas" title="AvantiGas">AvantiGas</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Shell_Gas" class="mw-redirect" title="Shell Gas">Shell Gas LPG</a>) is off the A6192 at junction 29A at <a href="/wiki/Duckmanton" title="Duckmanton">Duckmanton</a> in <a href="/wiki/Staveley,_Derbyshire" title="Staveley, Derbyshire">Staveley</a>. <a href="/wiki/Sandvik_Mining_and_Construction" class="mw-redirect" title="Sandvik Mining and Construction">Sandvik Mining and Construction</a> UK are on the Astron Business Park, Swadlincote, near Brunel Healthcare; Keystone Lintels and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Keylite&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Keylite (page does not exist)">Keylite</a> <a href="/wiki/Roof_window" title="Roof window">roof windows</a>, part of the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Keystone_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Keystone Group (page does not exist)">Keystone Group</a>, are nearby. <a href="/wiki/DSF_Refractories_%26_Minerals_Ltd" title="DSF Refractories &amp; Minerals Ltd">DSF Refractories &amp; Minerals</a> are the UK\'s last main <a href="/wiki/Refractory" title="Refractory">refractory</a> company at <a href="/wiki/Friden,_Derbyshire" title="Friden, Derbyshire">Friden</a> at the A515/A5012 (<a href="/wiki/Via_Gellia" title="Via Gellia">Via Gellia</a>) junction. Next to the A5, on the region boundary, at <a href="/wiki/Shawell" title="Shawell">Shawell</a> Leics is Redland (Lafarge Roofing until 2008) <a href="/wiki/Roof_tiles" title="Roof tiles">roof tile</a> factory. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Flowflex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Flowflex (page does not exist)">Flowflex</a> make <a href="/wiki/Compression_fitting" title="Compression fitting">compression fittings</a> in Buxton.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Finning-Caterpillar_at_Desford_-_geograph.org.uk_-_863588.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Finning-Caterpillar_at_Desford_-_geograph.org.uk_-_863588.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Caterpillar at Desford</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Caterpillar_Inc." title="Caterpillar Inc.">Caterpillar Building Construction Products</a> makes <a href="/wiki/Backhoe_loader" title="Backhoe loader">backhoe loaders</a>, <a href="/wiki/Loader_(equipment)" title="Loader (equipment)">wheel loaders</a>, <a href="/wiki/Telescopic_handler" title="Telescopic handler">telehandlers</a>, and mini <a href="/wiki/Excavator" title="Excavator">excavators</a>. <a href="/wiki/Caterpillar_Inc." title="Caterpillar Inc.">Caterpillar</a> on an <a href="/wiki/RAF_Desford" title="RAF Desford">old airfield</a> near <a href="/wiki/Desford" title="Desford">Desford</a>; the site is also used by <a href="/wiki/Massey_Ferguson" title="Massey Ferguson">Massey Ferguson</a> for their spares division factory. <a href="/wiki/TEREX_Pegson" title="TEREX Pegson">Terex Pegson</a> make mobile caterpillar-tracked <a href="/wiki/Crusher" title="Crusher">crushing machines</a> next to the railway in Coalville. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Dacrylate&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Dacrylate (page does not exist)">Dacrylate</a> make paint in Kirkby-in-Ashfield. <a href="/wiki/SAME_Deutz-Fahr" class="mw-redirect" title="SAME Deutz-Fahr">SAME Deutz-Fahr</a> UK, is a tractor manufacturer based in <a href="/wiki/Barby,_Northamptonshire" title="Barby, Northamptonshire">Barby</a> in west Northamptonshire near the M6 north of Daventry, owned by <a href="/wiki/Treviglio" title="Treviglio">Treviglio</a> of Italy. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Toyota_Material_Handling&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Toyota Material Handling (page does not exist)">Toyota Material Handling</a> UK is at <a href="/wiki/Old_Dalby" title="Old Dalby">Old Dalby</a> on a former <a href="/wiki/Army_Base_Repair_Organisation" title="Army Base Repair Organisation">ABRO</a> (previously <a href="/wiki/Royal_Electrical_and_Mechanical_Engineers" title="Royal Electrical and Mechanical Engineers">REME</a>) vehicle depot. The <a href="/wiki/Dorman_Long" title="Dorman Long">Dorman Long</a> engineering consultancy is at Higham Ferrers.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Building_pylons_At_Eakring_training_centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_279712.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Building_pylons_At_Eakring_training_centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_279712.jpg/220px-Building_pylons_At_Eakring_training_centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_279712.jpg" width="220" height="293" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Building_pylons_At_Eakring_training_centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_279712.jpg/330px-Building_pylons_At_Eakring_training_centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_279712.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Building_pylons_At_Eakring_training_centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_279712.jpg/440px-Building_pylons_At_Eakring_training_centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_279712.jpg 2x" data-file-width="480" data-file-height="640" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Building_pylons_At_Eakring_training_centre_-_geograph.org.uk_-_279712.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/National_Grid_plc" title="National Grid plc">National Grid plc</a> has its main <a href="/wiki/Ofsted" title="Ofsted">Ofsted</a>-checked <a href="/w/index.php?title=Eakring_Training_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Eakring Training Centre (page does not exist)">Eakring Training Centre</a> in Nottinghamshire, where trainees learn how to build <a href="/wiki/Transmission_tower" title="Transmission tower">electricity pylons</a>, including the new <a href="/w/index.php?title=T_pylon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="T pylon (page does not exist)">T pylon</a>; National Grid has other training sites in <a href="/wiki/Hollinwood,_Greater_Manchester" title="Hollinwood, Greater Manchester">Hollinwood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hitchin" title="Hitchin">Hitchin</a></div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Charles_Lawrence_International&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Charles Lawrence International (page does not exist)">Charles Lawrence International</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/Malcolm_Group" title="Malcolm Group">Malcolm Group</a>), on the Northern Road Industrial Estate in Newark makes <a href="/wiki/EPDM_rubber" title="EPDM rubber">EPDM rubber</a> granules and machinery for maintaining artificial sports surfaces. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Premier_Pitches&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Premier Pitches (page does not exist)">Premier Pitches</a> of <a href="/wiki/Nether_Handley" title="Nether Handley">Nether Handley</a>, off the <a href="/wiki/A6052_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A6052 road">A6052</a> at <a href="/wiki/Unstone" title="Unstone">Unstone</a> in northeast Derbyshire, made the pitch for Wembley Stadium, as well as for many other main pitches. Hewitt Sportsturf, just south of Whetstone next to the M1 in <a href="/wiki/Cosby,_Leicestershire" title="Cosby, Leicestershire">Cosby</a>, supplied the turf (360 rolls) for the <a href="/wiki/Olympic_Stadium_(London)" class="mw-redirect" title="Olympic Stadium (London)">Olympic Stadium</a> in March 2011, although it was grown near Scunthorpe; a division of the company, Petersfield Growing Mediums, which supplies compost, has a Royal Warrant. <a href="/wiki/Werner_Co." title="Werner Co.">Werner</a> UK (Britain\'s leading manufacturer of metal <a href="/wiki/Step_ladder" class="mw-redirect" title="Step ladder">step ladders</a>) moved its <a href="/wiki/ABRU" title="ABRU">ABRU</a> site, off the A6 in the south of Belper, to Essex in 2016. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Caunton_Engineering&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Caunton Engineering (page does not exist)">Caunton Engineering</a>, steel constructors, on the site of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Moorgreen_Colliery&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Moorgreen Colliery (page does not exist)">Moorgreen Colliery</a> in Eastwood built the Olympics <a href="/wiki/Water_Polo_Arena" title="Water Polo Arena">Water Polo Arena</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=PTS_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="PTS (company) (page does not exist)">PTS</a> (part of BSS) at Crick claims to be the main provider of supplies to UK plumbers. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Versalift&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Versalift (page does not exist)">Versalift</a> UK (van-mounted access platforms) are at Burton Latimer. <a href="/wiki/Omya" title="Omya">Omya</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Industrial_mineral" title="Industrial mineral">industrial minerals</a>) is between the A52 and railway at Derby.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Textiles_and_clothing">Textiles and clothing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Midlands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Textiles and clothing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Doctors_1460_Black_Worn.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Doctors_1460_Black_Worn.jpg/220px-Doctors_1460_Black_Worn.jpg" width="220" height="216" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Doctors_1460_Black_Worn.jpg/330px-Doctors_1460_Black_Worn.jpg 1.5x, class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Doctors_1460_Black_Worn.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Dr_Martens" class="mw-redirect" title="Dr Martens">Dr Martens</a> and many footwear companies are based in the south of the region, south-east of <a href="/wiki/Wellingborough" title="Wellingborough">Wellingborough</a>, at <a href="/wiki/Wollaston,_Northamptonshire" title="Wollaston, Northamptonshire">Wollaston</a></div></div></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_current_and_defunct_clothing_%26_footwear_stores_in_the_United_Kingdom" class="mw-redirect" title="List of current and defunct clothing &amp; footwear stores in the United Kingdom">List of current and defunct clothing &amp; footwear stores in the United Kingdom</a></div>\n<p>The fashion company <a href="/wiki/Paul_Smith_(fashion_designer)" title="Paul Smith (fashion designer)">Paul Smith</a> is in Lenton. The lingerie companies <a href="/wiki/Gossard" class="mw-redirect" title="Gossard">Gossard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aristoc" title="Aristoc">Aristoc</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pretty_Polly_(hosiery)" title="Pretty Polly (hosiery)">Pretty Polly</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Berlei" title="Berlei">Berlei</a> (formerly owned by <a href="/wiki/Courtaulds" title="Courtaulds">Courtaulds</a>, now CUK Clothing) are based in <a href="/wiki/Daybrook" title="Daybrook">Daybrook</a>; most of their hosiery is now made at West Mill in <a href="/wiki/Belper" title="Belper">Belper</a>. <a href="/wiki/Speedo_International_Limited" class="mw-redirect" title="Speedo International Limited">Speedo International Limited</a> is on the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ng2_business_park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ng2 business park (page does not exist)">ng2 business park</a> on Queens Drive (near Experian, formerly in <a href="/wiki/Bobbers_Mill" class="mw-redirect" title="Bobbers Mill">Bobbers Mill</a> on the <a href="/wiki/A610_road" title="A610 road">A610</a> near <a href="/wiki/Basford,_Nottingham" title="Basford, Nottingham">Basford</a> before 2010). Its <a href="/wiki/LZR_Racer" title="LZR Racer">LZR Racer</a> suit helped <a href="/wiki/Michael_Phelps" title="Michael Phelps">Michael Phelps</a> win eight golds at the <a href="/wiki/Swimming_at_the_2008_Summer_Olympics" title="Swimming at the 2008 Summer Olympics">2008 Olympics</a>. In Enderby, on the B582 close to the M69 and a large electricity substation, is <a href="/wiki/Next_(clothing)" class="mw-redirect" title="Next (clothing)">Next</a>, created by <a href="/wiki/George_Davies_(retailer)" title="George Davies (retailer)">George Davies</a> in 1981, which is the largest company in the region (and the Midlands) by number of employees with 59,000, and has the second largest turnover (\xc2\xa33&#160;billion) of companies headquartered in the region, after Boots (\xc2\xa36 billion).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (October 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Next_-_geograph.org.uk_-_491690.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Next_-_geograph.org.uk_-_491690.jpg/220px-Next_-_geograph.org.uk_-_491690.jpg" width="220" height="162" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Next_-_geograph.org.uk_-_491690.jpg/330px-Next_-_geograph.org.uk_-_491690.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Next_-_geograph.org.uk_-_491690.jpg/440px-Next_-_geograph.org.uk_-_491690.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="471" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Next_-_geograph.org.uk_-_491690.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Headquarters of Next Retailing in July 2007 at Enderby, next to the M69; the largest company by turnover in the Midlands</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Boden_(clothing)" title="Boden (clothing)">Boden (clothing)</a> is on the Meridian estate in Leicester. <a href="/wiki/Wolsey_(clothing)" title="Wolsey (clothing)">Wolsey (clothing)</a> is off the A563 in the northeast of Leicester, east of <a href="/wiki/Rushey_Mead" title="Rushey Mead">Rushey Mead</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Monarch_Knitting_Machinery&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Monarch Knitting Machinery (page does not exist)">Monarch Knitting Machinery</a> UK is in Beaumont Leys. Scott Nichol make traditional socks in Hinckley. <a href="/w/index.php?title=HJ_Hall&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="HJ Hall (page does not exist)">HJ Hall</a> of Hinckley are a larger company, who own <a href="/w/index.php?title=Pantherella&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Pantherella (page does not exist)">Pantherella</a>, who make socks in Leicester. <a href="/wiki/Per_Una" class="mw-redirect" title="Per Una">Per Una</a> have a factory near Cossington and the A46/A607 junction. Much of Britain\'s lingerie and hosiery is made in the region. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Crystal_Martin&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Crystal Martin (page does not exist)">Crystal Martin</a> UK make lingerie (for clothing chains) off the B6018 in the south of <a href="/wiki/Sutton-in-Ashfield" title="Sutton-in-Ashfield">Sutton-in-Ashfield</a>, near the A38 bypass. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wacoal_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Wacoal (company) (page does not exist)">Wacoal Europe</a> (former Eveden) makes lingerie on the B576 (former A6) in Desborough. Guilford Europe (former Guilford Kapwood), at Somercotes, makes fabric (<a href="/wiki/Warp_knitting" title="Warp knitting">warp knitting</a>) for sports clothing and automotive products, and have been owned by <a href="/wiki/Lear_Corporation" title="Lear Corporation">Lear Corporation</a> since 2012.\n</p><p>Many footwear companies such as <a href="/wiki/Shoe_Zone" title="Shoe Zone">Shoe Zone</a> (which bought out Stead and Simpson), are based in Leicester. <a href="/wiki/Brantano_Footwear" title="Brantano Footwear">Brantano Footwear UK</a>, based in Leicester before 2002, were in <a href="/wiki/Ellistown_and_Battleflat" title="Ellistown and Battleflat">Ellistown and Battleflat</a> until March 2017, just south of <a href="/wiki/Coalville" title="Coalville">Coalville</a> near M1 junction 22, nearby to <a href="/wiki/Nestl%C3%A9" title="Nestl\xc3\xa9">Nestl\xc3\xa9</a>\'s national distribution centre. <a href="/wiki/Loake" title="Loake">Loake</a> make shoes at Kettering, and have a Royal appointment. <a href="/wiki/Church%27s" title="Church&#39;s">Church\'s Shoes</a> are at Northampton are also high quality and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Barker_Shoes&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Barker Shoes (page does not exist)">Barker Shoes</a> are at Earls Barton. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Joseph_Cheaney_%26_Sons&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Joseph Cheaney &amp; Sons (page does not exist)">Joseph Cheaney &amp; Sons</a> are in Desborough near the Midland Main Line. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Tricker%27s&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Tricker&#39;s (page does not exist)">Tricker\'s</a> shoes in Northampton have a royal warrant. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Sanders_%26_Sanders&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sanders &amp; Sanders (page does not exist)">Sanders &amp; Sanders</a> and <a href="/wiki/Grenson" class="mw-redirect" title="Grenson">Grenson</a> make shoes in Rushden. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Jeffery_West&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Jeffery West (page does not exist)">Jeffery West</a> make shoes off the A4501 in Cliftonville, east Northampton, near <a href="/wiki/Northampton_General_Hospital" title="Northampton General Hospital">Northampton General Hospital</a> and the head office of <a href="/wiki/Local_government_in_Northampton" title="Local government in Northampton">Northampton Borough Council</a>. Off the A428 near the hospital is <a href="/wiki/Edward_Green_Shoes" title="Edward Green Shoes">Edward Green Shoes</a>. <a href="/wiki/Crockett_%26_Jones" title="Crockett &amp; Jones">Crockett &amp; Jones</a> make high-class shoes in the northeast of Northampton, towards Abington, and are the only main shoe factory left in the town. <a href="/wiki/Dr._Martens" title="Dr. Martens">Dr. Martens</a> were until 2003 made at Irthlingborough. The <a href="/wiki/BLC_Leather_Technology_Centre" title="BLC Leather Technology Centre">BLC Leather Technology Centre</a> is in Moulton and <a href="/wiki/SATRA" title="SATRA">SATRA</a>, in west Kettering, both conduct footwear research. Aspex make sports sunglasses in Moulton, near <a href="/wiki/Moulton_College" title="Moulton College">Moulton College</a>.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Telegraph_Poles,_Boston_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1206673.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Telegraph_Poles%2C_Boston_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1206673.jpg/220px-Telegraph_Poles%2C_Boston_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1206673.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Telegraph_Poles%2C_Boston_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1206673.jpg/330px-Telegraph_Poles%2C_Boston_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1206673.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Telegraph_Poles%2C_Boston_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1206673.jpg/440px-Telegraph_Poles%2C_Boston_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1206673.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Telegraph_Poles,_Boston_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1206673.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Calders_%26_Grandidge" title="Calders &amp; Grandidge">Calders &amp; Grandidge</a> in the south of Boston are the UK\'s largest supplier of <a href="/wiki/Utility_pole" title="Utility pole">telegraph poles</a> and wooden <a href="/wiki/Railroad_tie" title="Railroad tie">railway sleepers</a></div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hammonds_(furniture)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hammonds (furniture) (page does not exist)">Hammonds</a>, the furniture company, is in Hinckley. <a href="/wiki/Sports_Direct" title="Sports Direct">Sports Direct</a> is based in <a href="/wiki/Shirebrook" title="Shirebrook">Shirebrook</a> on an old <a href="/wiki/Bolsover" title="Bolsover">Bolsover</a> coal mine. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wade_Spring&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Wade Spring (page does not exist)">Wade Spring</a>, the UK\'s leading manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Upholstery" title="Upholstery">upholstery</a> springs, is in Long Eaton off the A6005; next-door at the Trent Business Centre is <a href="/wiki/Sunspel" title="Sunspel">Sunspel</a>, who introduced the <a href="/wiki/T-shirt" title="T-shirt">t-shirt</a> to the British market; nearby Meadowmead make premium furniture off the B6540, and <a href="/wiki/Aga_Rangemaster_Group" title="Aga Rangemaster Group">Aga Rangemaster Group</a> make kitchen <a href="/wiki/Sinks" class="mw-redirect" title="Sinks">sinks</a>; on the other side of railway <a href="/w/index.php?title=Gill_(clothing)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gill (clothing) (page does not exist)">Gill (clothing)</a>, who make marine clothing. <a href="/wiki/Duresta" title="Duresta">Duresta Upholstery</a> is in Long Eaton, with a factory of <a href="/wiki/DFS_(British_retailer)" class="mw-redirect" title="DFS (British retailer)">DFS</a> opposite. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Anstey_Wallpaper_Company&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Anstey Wallpaper Company (page does not exist)">Anstey Wallpaper Company</a> in Loughborough, makes high-end wallpaper, south of the town on the east side of the railway in the former Ladybird offices and factory. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Fogarty_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Fogarty (company) (page does not exist)">Fogarty (company)</a> make <a href="/wiki/Duvet" title="Duvet">duvets</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pillow" title="Pillow">pillows</a> in <a href="/wiki/Fishtoft" title="Fishtoft">Fishtoft</a>, Boston, next to <a href="/wiki/The_Haven,_Boston" title="The Haven, Boston">The Haven</a>. W&amp;G Sissons on the Chesterfield Est, now owned by <a href="/wiki/Franke_(company)" title="Franke (company)">Franke</a>, has been the UK\'s largest manufacturer of stainless steel sinks since the 1950s. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Leaderflush_Shapland&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Leaderflush Shapland (page does not exist)">Leaderflush Shapland</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/SIG_plc" title="SIG plc">SIG plc</a>) make doors near the A608/<a href="/wiki/A610_road" title="A610 road">A610</a> junction at <a href="/wiki/Aldercar_and_Langley_Mill" title="Aldercar and Langley Mill">Aldercar and Langley Mill</a>. <a href="/wiki/Parker_Knoll" title="Parker Knoll">Parker Knoll</a> make high-end furniture off the B6016 on the Greenhill Industrial Estate, south of Alfreton. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Greene,_Tweed&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Greene, Tweed (page does not exist)">Greene, Tweed</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Elastomer" title="Elastomer">elastomers</a>) is in Ruddington next to Experian. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Viaton&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Viaton (page does not exist)">Viaton</a> makes micronised <a href="/wiki/Baryte" title="Baryte">barytes</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hopton,_Derbyshire" title="Hopton, Derbyshire">Hopton</a>, Derbyshire. <a href="/wiki/Gunn_%26_Moore" title="Gunn &amp; Moore">Gunn &amp; Moore</a> (GM), off the A612 north of Trent Bridge cricket ground, is an exclusive <a href="/wiki/Cricket_bat" title="Cricket bat">cricket bat</a> manufacturer.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lea_Bridge_-_John_Smedley_Mill_-_Factory_Shop.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Lea_Bridge_-_John_Smedley_Mill_-_Factory_Shop.jpg/220px-Lea_Bridge_-_John_Smedley_Mill_-_Factory_Shop.jpg" width="220" height="168" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Lea_Bridge_-_John_Smedley_Mill_-_Factory_Shop.jpg/330px-Lea_Bridge_-_John_Smedley_Mill_-_Factory_Shop.jpg 1.5x,
